<h1 _ngcontent-fhg-c119="" class="doc-title ng-star-inserted" title="functionalButtonComponentManager(场景化融合Button组件管理)"> functionalButtonComponentManager(场景化融合Button组件管理) </h1>

<div _ngcontent-fhg-c106="" auitextselectionexpansion="" class="markdown-body ng-star-inserted renderOptimization" style="position: relative;"> <div><p>本模块提供Button组件的逻辑管理，辅助HarmonyOS应用和元服务通过Button组件完成相应功能。</p> <p><strong>模型约束：</strong>此接口仅可在Stage模型下使用。</p> device-type="phone,tablet,tv,2in1">FunctionalButtonController<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section942719311715" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2><div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span></div><p>FunctionalButton组件控制器，用来回调组件内部的点击事件。</p> <p><strong>模型约束：</strong>此接口仅可在Stage模型下使用。</p> <p><strong>元服务API：</strong>从版本4.1.0(11)开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p> <p><strong>系统能力</strong><strong>：</strong>SystemCapability.AtomicserviceComponent.UIComponent</p> <p><strong>起始版本：</strong>4.1.0(11)</p> </div> <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 2113px;"><h3 id="section356683016304" device-type="phone,tablet,tv,2in1" class="firsth2">onGetPhoneNumber<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section356683016304" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3><div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span></div><p>onGetPhoneNumber(callback: AsyncCallback&lt;GetPhoneNumberResult&gt;): FunctionalButtonController</p> <p>注册FunctionalButton组件为快速验证手机号的点击事件，使用callback异步回调。</p> <p>该接口功能依赖Account Kit，参见<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/account-api-authentication#section610319714214" target="_blank">createAuthorizationWithHuaweiIDRequest</a>。</p> <p><strong>模型约束：</strong>此接口仅可在Stage模型下使用。</p> <p><strong>元服务API：</strong>从版本4.1.0(11)开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p> <p><strong>系统能力</strong><strong>：</strong>SystemCapability.AtomicserviceComponent.UIComponent</p> <p><strong>设备行为差异：</strong>对于4.1.0(11)版本，该接口在Phone、Tablet、2in1中可正常调用，在其他设备类型中返回801错误码。对于5.1.0(18)及之后版本，该接口在Phone、Tablet、2in1、TV中可正常调用，在其他设备类型中返回801错误码。</p> <p><strong>起始版本：</strong>4.1.0(11)</p> <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table><thead><tr><th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.32.11.1.5.1.1" width="10%"><p>参数名</p> </th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.32.11.1.5.1.2" width="40%"><p>类型</p> </th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.32.11.1.5.1.3" width="10%"><p>必填</p> </th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.32.11.1.5.1.4" width="40%"><p>说明</p> </th> </tr> </thead> <tbody><tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="10%"><p>callback</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="40%"><p>AsyncCallback&lt;<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/scenario-fusion-functionalbuttoncomponentmanager#section593445861420">GetPhoneNumberResult</a>&gt;</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="10%"><p>是</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="40%"><p>回调函数。当获取电话号码成功，err为undefined，data为获取到的账号用户的临时登录凭证（Authorization Code）；否则为错误对象。</p> <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content"><p>可通过临时登录凭证获取真实手机号，临时登录凭证时效5分钟，具体操作可参考“<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/account-get-phonenumber#section380015370555" target="_blank">服务端开发</a>”章节。</p> </div></div></div> </td> </tr>  </tbody></table></div> </div> <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t"> <tbody><tr class="firstRow"><th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.32.13.1.3.1.1" width="50%"><p>类型</p> </th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.32.13.1.3.1.2" width="50%"><p>说明</p> </th> </tr><tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/scenario-fusion-functionalbuttoncomponentmanager#section942719311715">FunctionalButtonController</a></p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/scenario-fusion-functionalbutton#section1753203873911">FunctionalButton</a>组件控制器。</p> </td> </tr>  </tbody></table></div> </div> <p><strong>示例：</strong></p> <div _ngcontent-fhg-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-fhg-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div device-type="phone,tablet,tv,2in1">onGetRealtimePhoneNumber<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section1136212296301" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3><div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span></div><p>onGetRealtimePhoneNumber(callback: AsyncCallback&lt;GetRealtimePhoneNumberResult&gt;): FunctionalButtonController</p> <p>注册FunctionalButton组件为实时验证手机号的点击事件，使用callback异步回调。</p> <p>该接口功能依赖Account Kit，参见<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/account-api-authentication#section610319714214" target="_blank">createAuthorizationWithHuaweiIDRequest</a>。</p> <p><strong>模型约束：</strong>此接口仅可在Stage模型下使用。</p> <p><strong>元服务API：</strong>从版本4.1.0(11)开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p> <p><strong>系统能力</strong><strong>：</strong>SystemCapability.AtomicserviceComponent.UIComponent</p> <p><strong>设备行为差异：</strong>对于4.1.0(11)版本，该接口在Phone、Tablet、2in1中可正常调用，在其他设备类型中返回801错误码。对于5.1.0(18)及之后版本，该接口在Phone、Tablet、2in1、TV中可正常调用，在其他设备类型中返回801错误码。</p> <p><strong>起始版本：</strong>4.1.0(11)</p> <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table><thead><tr><th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.33.11.1.5.1.1" width="21.11%"><p>参数名</p> </th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.33.11.1.5.1.2" width="28.89%"><p>类型</p> </th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.33.11.1.5.1.3" width="10%"><p>必填</p> </th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.33.11.1.5.1.4" width="40%"><p>说明</p> </th> </tr> </thead> <tbody><tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="21.11%"><p>callback</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="28.89%"><p>AsyncCallback&lt;<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/scenario-fusion-functionalbuttoncomponentmanager#section1617620229162">GetRealtimePhoneNumberResult</a>&gt;</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="10%"><p>是</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="40%"><p>回调函数。当获取实时电话号码成功，err为undefined，data为获取到的账号用户的临时登录凭证（Authorization Code）；否则为错误对象。</p> <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content"><p>可通过临时登录凭证获取真实手机号，临时登录凭证时效5分钟，具体操作可参考“<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/account-get-phonenumber#section380015370555" target="_blank">服务端开发</a>”章节。</p> </div></div></div> </td> </tr>  </tbody></table></div> </div> <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t"> <tbody><tr class="firstRow"><th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.33.13.1.3.1.1" width="50%"><p>类型</p> </th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.33.13.1.3.1.2" width="50%"><p>说明</p> </th> </tr><tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/scenario-fusion-functionalbuttoncomponentmanager#section942719311715">FunctionalButtonController</a></p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/scenario-fusion-functionalbutton#section1753203873911">FunctionalButton</a>组件控制器。</p> </td> </tr>  </tbody></table></div> </div> class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section5733430102618" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3><div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span></div><p>onLaunchApp(callback: AsyncCallback&lt;void&gt;): FunctionalButtonController</p> <p>注册FunctionalButton组件为打开APP的点击事件，使用callback异步回调。</p> <p>该接口功能依赖Ability Kit，参见<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-inner-application-uiabilitycontext#startability" target="_blank">startAbility</a>。</p> <p><strong>模型约束：</strong>此接口仅可在Stage模型下使用。</p> <p><strong>元服务API：</strong>从版本4.1.0(11)开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p> <p><strong>系统能力</strong><strong>：</strong>SystemCapability.AtomicserviceComponent.UIComponent</p> <p><strong>设备行为差异：</strong>对于4.1.0(11)版本，该接口在Phone、Tablet、2in1中可正常调用，在其他设备类型中返回801错误码。对于5.1.0(18)及之后版本，该接口在Phone、Tablet、2in1、TV中可正常调用，在其他设备类型中返回801错误码。</p> <p><strong>起始版本：</strong>4.1.0(11)</p> <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1977px;"><h3 id="section1677571515229" device-type="phone,tablet,tv,2in1">onOpenSetting<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section1677571515229" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3><div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span></div><p>onOpenSetting(callback: AsyncCallback&lt;OpenSettingResult&gt;): FunctionalButtonController</p> <p>注册FunctionalButton组件为打开授权设置页的点击事件，使用callback异步回调。</p> <p>该接口功能依赖Ability Kit，参见<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-inner-application-uiabilitycontext#startabilityforresult" target="_blank">startAbilityForResult</a>。</p> <p><strong>模型约束：</strong>此接口仅可在Stage模型下使用。</p> <p><strong>元服务API：</strong>从版本4.1.0(11)开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p> <p><strong>系统能力</strong><strong>：</strong>SystemCapability.AtomicserviceComponent.UIComponent</p> <p><strong>设备行为差异：</strong>对于4.1.0(11)版本，该接口在Phone、Tablet、2in1中可正常调用，在其他设备类型中返回801错误码。对于5.1.0(18)及之后版本，该接口在Phone、Tablet、2in1、TV中可正常调用，在其他设备类型中返回801错误码。</p> <p><strong>起始版本：</strong>4.1.0(11)</p> <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table><thead><tr><th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.35.11.1.5.1.1" width="13.48%"><p>参数名</p> </th> <th </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="40%"><p>回调函数。当打开授权设置页成功，err为undefined，data为打开设置成功时返回的响应；否则为错误对象。</p> </td> </tr>  </tbody></table></div> </div> <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>  <div id="section15593431203020" device-type="phone,tablet,tv,2in1">onChooseAvatar<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon class="support-device-item">TV</span></div><p>onChooseAvatar(callback: AsyncCallback&lt;ChooseAvatarResult&gt;): FunctionalButtonController</p> <p>注册FunctionalButton组件为选择头像的点击事件，使用callback异步回调。</p> <p><strong>模型约束：</strong>此接口仅可在Stage模型下使用。</p> <p><strong>元服务API：</strong>从版本4.1.0(11)开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p> <p><strong>系统能力</strong><strong>：</strong>SystemCapability.AtomicserviceComponent.UIComponent</p> <p><strong>设备行为差异：</strong>该接口在Phone、Tablet、2in1中可正常调用，在其他设备类型中返回801错误码。</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="40%"><p>回调函数。当选择头像调用成功，err为undefined，data为选择头像成功时返回的所选头像图片的地址；否则为错误对象。</p> <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section01098275512" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3><div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span></div><p>onChooseAddress(callback: AsyncCallback&lt;ChooseAddressResult&gt;): FunctionalButtonController</p> <p>注册FunctionalButton组件为选择收货地址的点击事件，使用callback异步回调。</p> <p>该接口功能依赖Account Kit，参见<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/account-choose-address#section0668846105912" target="_blank">chooseAddress</a>。</p> <p><strong>模型约束：</strong>此接口仅可在Stage模型下使用。</p> <p><strong>元服务API：</strong>从版本5.0.0(12)开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p> <p><strong>系统能力</strong><strong>：</strong>SystemCapability.AtomicserviceComponent.UIComponent</p> <p><strong>设备行为差异：</strong>该接口在Phone、Tablet、2in1中可正常调用，在其他设备类型中返回801错误码。</p> <p><strong>起始版本：</strong>5.0.0(12)</p> <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table><thead><tr><th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.37.11.1.5.1.1" width="10%"><p>必填</p> </th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.37.11.1.5.1.4" width="40%"><p>说明</p> </th> </tr> </thead> <tbody><tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="12.08%"><p>callback</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="37.92%"><p>AsyncCallback&lt;<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/scenario-fusion-functionalbuttoncomponentmanager#section176651720152015">ChooseAddressResult</a>&gt;</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="10%"><p>是</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="40%"><p>回调函数。当选择收货地址点击成功，err为undefined，data为选择收货地址的返回结果；否则为错误对象。</p> </td> </tr>  </tbody></table></div> </div> <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t"> <tbody><tr class="firstRow"><th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.37.13.1.3.1.1" width="50%"><p>类型</p> </th> device-type="phone,tablet,tv,2in1">onChooseInvoiceTitle<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section1313901101117" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3><div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span></div><p>onChooseInvoiceTitle(callback: AsyncCallback&lt;ChooseInvoiceTitleResult&gt;): FunctionalButtonController</p> <p>注册FunctionalButton组件为选择发票抬头的点击事件，使用callback异步回调。</p> <p>该接口功能依赖Account Kit，参见<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/account-api-invoiceassistant#section162103412610" target="_blank">selectInvoiceTitle</a>。</p> <p><strong>模型约束：</strong>此接口仅可在Stage模型下使用。</p> <p><strong>元服务API：</strong>从版本5.0.0(12)开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p> <p><strong>系统能力</strong><strong>：</strong>SystemCapability.AtomicserviceComponent.UIComponent</p> <p><strong>设备行为差异：</strong>该接口在Phone、Tablet、2in1中可正常调用，在其他设备类型中返回801错误码。</p> <p><strong>起始版本：</strong>5.0.0(12)</p> <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table><thead><tr><th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.38.11.1.5.1.1" device-type="phone,tablet,tv,2in1">onRealNameAuthentication<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section10375238132610" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3><div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span></div><p>onRealNameAuthentication(callback: AsyncCallback&lt;RealNameAuthenticationResult&gt;): FunctionalButtonController</p> <p>注册FunctionalButton组件为实名信息校验的点击事件，使用callback异步回调。</p> <p>该接口功能依赖Account Kit，参见<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/account-api-authentication#section164113311433" target="_blank">executeRequest</a>。</p> <p><strong>模型约束：</strong>此接口仅可在Stage模型下使用。</p> <p><strong>元服务API：</strong>从版本5.0.0(12)开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p> <p><strong>系统能力</strong><strong>：</strong>SystemCapability.AtomicserviceComponent.UIComponent</p> <p><strong>设备行为差异：</strong>该接口在Phone、Tablet中可正常调用，在其他设备类型中返回1001500003错误码。</p> <p><strong>起始版本：</strong>5.0.0(12)</p> <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table><thead><tr><th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.39.11.1.5.1.1" id="mcps1.3.39.11.1.5.1.3" width="7.28%"><p>必填</p> </th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.39.11.1.5.1.4" width="42.730000000000004%"><p>说明</p> </th> </tr> </thead> <tbody><tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="10%"><p>callback</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="39.989999999999995%"><p>AsyncCallback&lt;<a </tbody></table></div> </div> <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t"> <tbody><tr class="firstRow"><th align="left" id="section1646722611424" device-type="phone,tablet,tv,2in1">onFaceAuthentication<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section1646722611424" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3><div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span></div><p>onFaceAuthentication(callback: AsyncCallback&lt;FaceAuthenticationResult&gt;): FunctionalButtonController</p> <p>注册FunctionalButton组件为人脸核身的点击事件，使用callback异步回调。</p> <p>该接口功能依赖Account Kit，参见<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/account-api-authentication#section610319714214" target="_blank">createAuthorizationWithHuaweiIDRequest</a>，<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/account-api-authentication#section620452019185" target="_blank">AuthenticationController</a>，<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/account-api-authentication#section164113311433" target="_blank">executeRequest</a>。</p> <p><strong>模型约束：</strong>此接口仅可在Stage模型下使用。</p> <p><strong>元服务API：</strong>从版本5.0.0(12)开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p> <p><strong>系统能力</strong><strong>：</strong>SystemCapability.AtomicserviceComponent.UIComponent</p> <p><strong>设备行为差异：</strong>该接口在Phone、Tablet中可正常调用，在其他设备类型中返回1001500003错误码。</p> <p><strong>起始版本：</strong>5.0.0(12)</p> <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table><thead><tr><th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.40.11.1.5.1.1" width="10%"><p>参数名</p> </th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.40.11.1.5.1.2" width="37.31%"><p>类型</p> </th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.40.11.1.5.1.3" width="6.510000000000001%"><p>必填</p> </th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.40.11.1.5.1.4" width="46.18%"><p>说明</p> </th> </tr> </thead> <tbody><tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="10%"><p>callback</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="37.31%"><p>AsyncCallback&lt;<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/scenario-fusion-functionalbuttoncomponentmanager#section955010367519">FaceAuthenticationResult</a>&gt;</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="6.510000000000001%"><p>是</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="46.18%"><p>回调函数。当人脸认证成功，err为undefined，data为获取到的人脸认证对应的返回体：authCode、openID；否则为错误对象。</p> </td> </tr>  </tbody></table></div> </div> <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t"> <tbody><tr class="firstRow"><th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.40.13.1.3.1.1" width="48.68%"><p>类型</p> </th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.40.13.1.3.1.2" width="51.32%"><p>说明</p> </th> </tr><tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="48.68%"><p><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/scenario-fusion-functionalbuttoncomponentmanager#section942719311715">FunctionalButtonController</a></p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="51.32%"><p><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/scenario-fusion-functionalbutton#section1753203873911">FunctionalButton</a>组件控制器。</p> </td> </tr>  </tbody></table></div> </div> <p><strong>示例：</strong></p> <div _ngcontent-fhg-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-fhg-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div device-type="phone,tablet,tv,2in1">onFaceVerification<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section487002034718" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3><div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span></div><p>onFaceVerification(verifyToken: string, callback: AsyncCallback&lt;FaceVerificationResult&gt;): void</p> <p>注册FunctionalButton组件为人脸验证的点击事件，使用callback异步回调。</p> <p>该接口功能依赖Account Kit，参见<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/account-api-authentication#section610319714214" target="_blank">createAuthorizationWithHuaweiIDRequest</a>，<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/account-api-authentication#section620452019185" target="_blank">AuthenticationController</a>，<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/account-api-authentication#section164113311433" target="_blank">executeRequest</a>。</p> <p><strong>模型约束：</strong>此接口仅可在Stage模型下使用。</p> <p><strong>元服务API：</strong>从版本5.0.0(12)开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p> <p><strong>系统能力</strong><strong>：</strong>SystemCapability.AtomicserviceComponent.UIComponent</p> <p><strong>设备行为差异：</strong>该接口在Phone、Tablet中可正常调用，在其他设备类型中返回1001500003错误码。</p> <p><strong>起始版本：</strong>5.0.0(12)</p> <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table><thead><tr><th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.41.11.1.5.1.1" width="10%"><p>参数名</p> </th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.41.11.1.5.1.2" width="34.2%"><p>类型</p> </th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.41.11.1.5.1.3" width="6.81%"><p>必填</p> </th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.41.11.1.5.1.4" width="48.99%"><p>说明</p> </th> </tr> </thead> <tbody><tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="10%"><p>verifyToken</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="34.2%"><p>string</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="6.81%"><p>是</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="48.99%"><p>验证成功的idToken，三方应用拉起华为账号客户端人脸验证页面时传入此Token，供华为账号客户端校验验证结果。</p> </td> </tr> <tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="10%"><p>callback</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="34.2%"><p>AsyncCallback&lt;<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/scenario-fusion-functionalbuttoncomponentmanager#section10953282537">FaceVerificationResult</a>&gt;</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="6.81%"><p>是</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="48.99%"><p>回调函数。当人脸验证点击成功，err为undefined，data为人脸验证的返回结果；否则为错误对象。</p> </td> </tr>  </tbody></table></div> </div> device-type="phone,tablet,tv,2in1">onChooseLocation<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section19781104631718" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3><div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span></div><p>onChooseLocation(callback: AsyncCallback&lt;ChooseLocationResult&gt;): FunctionalButtonController</p> <p>注册FunctionalButton组件为打开地图选点的点击事件，使用callback异步回调。</p> <p>该接口功能依赖Map Kit，参见<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/map-scenemap#section927375116348" target="_blank">chooseLocation</a>。</p> <p><strong>模型约束：</strong>此接口仅可在Stage模型下使用。</p> <p><strong>元服务API：</strong>从版本5.0.0(12)开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p> <p><strong>系统能力</strong><strong>：</strong>SystemCapability.AtomicserviceComponent.UIComponent</p> <p><strong>设备行为差异：</strong>对于5.0.0(12)版本，该接口在Phone、Tablet中可正常调用，在其他设备类型中返回801错误码。对于5.0.1(13)及之后版本，该接口在Phone、Tablet、2in1中可正常调用，在其他设备类型中返回801错误码。</p> <p><strong>起始版本：</strong>5.0.0(12)</p> <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table><thead><tr><th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.42.11.1.5.1.1" width="10%"><p>参数名</p> </th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.42.11.1.5.1.4" width="41.660000000000004%"><p>说明</p> </th> </tr> </thead> <tbody><tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="10%"><p>callback</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="40%"><p>AsyncCallback&lt;<a <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t"> <tbody><tr class="firstRow"><th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.42.13.1.3.1.1" AsyncCallback&lt;SubscribeLiveViewResult&gt;): FunctionalButtonController</p> <p>注册FunctionalButton组件为实况窗订阅的点击事件，使用callback异步回调。</p> <p><strong>模型约束：</strong>此接口仅可在Stage模型下使用。</p> <p><strong>系统能力</strong><strong>：</strong>SystemCapability.AtomicserviceComponent.UIComponent</p> <p><strong>设备行为差异：</strong>该接口在Phone、Tablet中可正常调用，在其他设备类型中返回801错误码。</p> id="section644174220486" device-type="phone,tablet,tv,2in1">onPermissionSetting<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section644174220486" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3><div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span></div><p>onPermissionSetting(callback: AsyncCallback&lt;PermissionSettingResult&gt;): FunctionalButtonController</p> <p>注册FunctionalButton组件为权限设置的点击事件，使用callback异步回调。</p> <p>该接口功能依赖Ability Kit，参见<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-abilityaccessctrl#requestpermissiononsetting12" target="_blank">requestPermissionOnSetting</a>。</p> <p><strong>模型约束：</strong>此接口仅可在Stage模型下使用。</p> <p><strong>元服务API：</strong>从版本5.0.2(14)开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p> <p><strong>系统能力</strong><strong>：</strong>SystemCapability.AtomicserviceComponent.UIComponent</p> <p><strong>设备行为差异：</strong>对于5.0.2(14)版本，该接口在Phone、Tablet、2in1中可正常调用，在其他设备类型中返回801错误码。对于5.1.0(18)及之后版本，该接口在Phone、Tablet、2in1、TV中可正常调用，在其他设备类型中返回801错误码。</p> <p><strong>起始版本：</strong>5.0.2(14)</p> <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table><thead><tr><th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.44.11.1.5.1.1" width="13.48%"><p>参数名</p> </th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.44.11.1.5.1.2" width="36.52%"><p>类型</p> </th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.44.11.1.5.1.3" width="10%"><p>必填</p> </th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.44.11.1.5.1.4" width="40%"><p>说明</p> </th> </tr> </thead> <tbody><tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="13.48%"><p>callback</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="36.52%"><p>AsyncCallback&lt;<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/scenario-fusion-functionalbuttoncomponentmanager#section1624725342">PermissionSettingResult</a>&gt;</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="10%"><p>是</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="40%"><p>回调函数。当权限设置点击成功，err为undefined，data为获取到的权限设置返回结果；否则为错误对象。</p> </td> </tr>  </tbody></table></div> </div> <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t"> <tbody><tr class="firstRow"><th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.44.13.1.3.1.1" width="50%"><p>类型</p> </th> <th href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/scenario-fusion-functionalbutton#section1753203873911">FunctionalButton</a>组件控制器。</p> </td> </tr>  </tbody></table></div> </div> auto 2021px;"><h3 id="section746185064513" device-type="phone,tablet,tv,2in1">onRequestSubscribeMessage<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section746185064513" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3><div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span></div><p>onRequestSubscribeMessage(callback: AsyncCallback&lt;RequestSubscribeMessageResult&gt;): FunctionalButtonController</p> <p>注册FunctionalButton组件为服务动态授权码按钮的点击事件，使用callback异步回调。</p> <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content"><p>该接口在元服务中可正常使用，在其他场景中返回10006、10008错误码。</p> </div></div></div> <p><strong>模型约束：</strong>此接口仅可在Stage模型下使用。</p> <p><strong>元服务API：</strong>从版本6.0.0(20)开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p> <p><strong>系统能力</strong><strong>：</strong>SystemCapability.AtomicserviceComponent.UIComponent</p> <p><strong>设备行为差异：</strong>该接口在Phone、Tablet中可正常调用，在其他设备类型中返回801错误码。</p> <p><strong>起始版本：</strong>6.0.0(20)</p> <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table><thead><tr><th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.45.11.1.5.1.1" width="13.48%"><p>参数名</p> </th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.45.11.1.5.1.2" width="36.52%"><p>类型</p> </th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.45.11.1.5.1.3" width="10%"><p>必填</p> </th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.45.11.1.5.1.4" width="40%"><p>说明</p> </th> </tr> </thead> <tbody><tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="13.48%"><p>callback</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="36.52%"><p>AsyncCallback&lt;<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/scenario-fusion-functionalbuttoncomponentmanager#section2076213310277">RequestSubscribeMessageResult</a>&gt;</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="10%"><p>是</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="40%"><p>回调函数。当服务动态授权码按钮点击成功，err为undefined，data为获取到的code返回结果；否则为错误对象。</p> </td> </tr>  </tbody></table></div> </div> <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t"> <tbody><tr class="firstRow"><th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.45.13.1.3.1.1" href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/scenario-fusion-functionalbuttoncomponentmanager#section942719311715">FunctionalButtonController</a></p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p><a <p><strong>元服务API：</strong>从版本6.0.0(20)开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p> <p><strong>系统能力</strong><strong>：</strong>SystemCapability.AtomicserviceComponent.UIComponent</p> device-type="phone,tablet,tv,2in1">onFeedback<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" FunctionalButtonController</p> <p>注册FunctionalButton组件为反馈按钮的点击事件，使用callback异步回调。</p> <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content"><p>仅提供给元服务使用。</p> </div></div></div> <p><strong>模型约束：</strong>此接口仅可在Stage模型下使用。</p> <p><strong>元服务API：</strong>从版本6.0.0(20)开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p> class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span></div><p>fontWeight(value: string | number | FontWeight): ButtonConfig</p> <p>设置FunctionalButton的字体粗细属性。</p> <p><strong>模型约束：</strong>此接口仅可在Stage模型下使用。</p> <p><strong>元服务API：</strong>从版本4.1.0(11)开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p> <p><strong>系统能力</strong><strong>：</strong>SystemCapability.AtomicserviceComponent.UIComponent</p> <p><strong>起始版本：</strong>4.1.0(11)</p> <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table><thead><tr><th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.53.9.1.5.1.1" width="15%"><p>参数名</p> </th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.53.9.1.5.1.2" <td class="cellrowborder" width="52.42%"><p>设置文本的字体粗细，number类型取值[100, 900]，取值间隔为100，默认为400，取值越大，字体越粗。string类型仅支持number类型取值的字符串形式，例如"400"，以及"bold"，"bolder"，"lighter"，"regular"，"medium"，"normal"，分别对应FontWeight中相应的枚举值。</p> <p>默认值：FontWeight.Normal</p> </td> </tr> class="tbBox"><table><thead><tr><th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.64.9.1.5.1.1" width="15%"><p>参数名</p> </th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.64.9.1.5.1.2" href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-types#sizeoptions" target="_blank">SizeOptions</a> | <a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-appendix-enums#imagesize" target="_blank">ImageSize</a></p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="10%"><p>是</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="45%"><p>设置背景图像的高度和宽度。当输入为{width: Length, height: Length}对象时，如果只设置一个属性，则第二个属性保持图片原始宽高比进行调整。默认保持原图的比例不变。</p> <p>width和height取值范围： [0, +∞)</p> <p>默认值：ImageSize.Auto</p> <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content"><p>设置为小于0的值时，按值为0显示。当设置了height未设置width时，width根据图片原始宽高比进行调整。</p> </div></div></div> </td> </tr> <p><strong>系统能力</strong><strong>：</strong>SystemCapability.AtomicserviceComponent.UIComponent</p> <p><strong>起始版本：</strong>4.1.0(11)</p> <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div _ngcontent-fhg-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-fhg-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-fhg-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div class="hljs-attr">x</span>: <span class="hljs-number">0</span>,</li><li>  <span class="hljs-attr">y</span>: <span class="hljs-number">0</span></li><li>}</li></ol></pre></div></div> href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-types#resourcecolor" target="_blank">ResourceColor</a></p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="10%"><p>是</p> </td> <td </td> </tr>  </tbody></table></div> </div> <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t"> <tbody><tr class="firstRow"><th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.78.11.1.3.1.1" width="50%"><p>类型</p> </th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.78.11.1.3.1.2" width="50%"><p>说明</p> </th> </tr><tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/scenario-fusion-functionalbuttoncomponentmanager#section8718135610381">ButtonConfig</a></p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p>ButtonConfig对象。</p> </td> </tr>  </tbody></table></div> </div> </div> <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 936px;"><h3 <p>设置FunctionalButton中的LoadingProgress图标的宽度属性。</p> <p><strong>模型约束：</strong>此接口仅可在Stage模型下使用。</p> <p><strong>元服务API：</strong>从版本4.1.0(11)开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p> <p><strong>系统能力</strong><strong>：</strong>SystemCapability.AtomicserviceComponent.UIComponent</p> <p><strong>起始版本：</strong>4.1.0(11)</p> <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table><thead><tr><th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.79.9.1.5.1.1" width="15%"><p>参数名</p> </th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.79.9.1.5.1.2" class="cellrowborder" width="45%"><p>设置图标自身的宽度。默认值：20，单位：vp。</p> <p>取值范围：(-∞, +∞)</p> <p>填写为负数时，宽度不超过按钮大小；填写正数时，宽度不受限于按钮大小，请合理填写数值。</p> <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content"><p><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-loadingprogress" href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/scenario-fusion-functionalbuttoncomponentmanager#section08531112317">loadingHeight</a>中的最小值。</p> </div></div></div> </td> </tr>  </tbody></table></div>
